beginSubroutine: s32'CmnCutSceneDamage_Kakusei'
  ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'pot'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    debugLogForScript: s32'pot', 0, 0
  endIf: 
  ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'fau'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    debugLogForScript: s32'fau', 0, 0
  endIf: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'CPUEstimate'
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'OnFrameStep'
  callSubroutine: s32'cmnOnFrameStep'
  if: Mem(PlayerVal0)
    modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(PgObjReg3), Val(1)
    modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(-1)
    ifNot: Mem(PlayerVal0)
      resetMaterialSet: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  if: Mem(PlayerVal6)
    if: Mem(BattleDoing)
      ifNot: Mem(IsSomebodysCutScene)
        ifNot: Mem(IsRoundTimerStop)
          ifNot: Mem(CheckStop)
            modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(PlayerVal6), Val(-1)
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    ifNot: Mem(PlayerVal5)
      storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal6), Val(0)
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'OnGuard'
  if: Mem(PlayerVal0)
    resetMaterialSet: 
    storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(0)
  endIf: 
  callSubroutine: s32'cmnOnGuard'
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'OnDamage'
  callSubroutine: s32'cmnOnDamage'
  storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(0)
  storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal3), Val(0)
  if: Mem(PlayerVal0)
    resetMaterialSet: 
    storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(0)
  endIf: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'OnLanding'
  callSubroutine: s32'cmnJumpCheck'
  storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(0)
  storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal3), Val(0)
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'OnDie'
  callSubroutine: s32'cmnOnDie'
endSubroutine:

beginState: s32'WallRun'
  upon: (IMMEDIATE)
    autoAirTurn: 1

    enableRomanCancelMove: 1
    counterHitUkeru: 0
    recoveryState: 
    isObjectActive: (STACK0)
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      sendSignal: (STACK0), (SIGNAL1)
    endIf: 
    isObjectActive: (STACK1)
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      sendSignal: (STACK1), (SIGNAL4)
    endIf: 
    isObjectActive: (STACK2)
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      sendSignal: (STACK2), (SIGNAL1)
    endIf: 
    ifNot: Mem(ObjReg3)
      checkLastStateName: s32'HaritsukiR_wall'
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        storeValue: Mem(ObjReg0), Val(1)
        if: Mem(ObjReg2)
          storeValue: Mem(ObjReg2), Val(0)
          storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
      else: 
        storeValue: Mem(ObjReg0), Val(0)
        if: Mem(ObjReg2)
          storeValue: Mem(ObjReg2), Val(0)
          storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
        endIf: 
      endElse: 
    endIf: 
    else: 
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)

    pushboxFix: 1
    addWhiffCancelOption: s32'WallRun_6P'

    autoAirTurn: 1
